CHE NAS BSTAN PA DANG SEMS CAN GYI DON DU YUN RING POR BZHUGS
DGOS PA'I GSOL BA BTAB PAS, BRAG DGON DU SKYE BRTAG

@083B GNANG BA'I LO RGYUS SOGS GSUNG ZHING, NGA LO DON DRUG PA
YIN PAS, DA YUN RING SDOD AE THUB MI SHES ZHES ZHAL GYIS BZHES
PA MA BYUNG, SKU SKYE BA GANG DU BZHES ZHUS PAR YANG, SNGAR
SLOB GNYER MUS LA RI KHROD NYAG BSKYANGS NAS SGRUB PA ZHIG
BYED

RGYU BYUNG NA DAG PA'I ZHING GCIG TU SKYE AE THUB KYI 'DUN PA
YIN NA'ANG, BAR DU RNAM G-YENG DANG DKOR GYI DBANG GIS RANG
DBANG 'DUS PA ZHIG DKA' BAR 'DUG KYANG, RGYA HOR DBUS GTZANG
SOGS SU SKYE BA LEN 'DOD NI MED CES BKA' PHEBS, DE YANG

THUGS RANG DBANG MI 'DUS PA GSUNG BA NI DGONGS PA CAN DU
MNGON, HOR ZLA BDUN PA'I NANG DU AAR SA LANG MI BZANG DANG
BCAS JO MJAL LA 'ONG, RJE 'DI NYID MJAL TE, LEGS NYES KYI
BRTAG PA ZHU BA DANG, ZANG ZING GI 'BUL NOD MANG DU BYAS,

DAM SEL GYI RNAM PAS NAM MKHA' SHIN TU 'TSUB CING, KHYAD PAR
DGE 'PHEL GYI RI RGYUD NAS SNA DRANGS, PHA BONG KHA'I BAR SER
BA DRAG TU BABS, DE 'PHRAL BSKANG BSHAGS DANG GTOR 'BUL SOGS
MDZAD PAS NAM MKHA' DVANGS, BRTAG PA YANG, AAR

SA LANG PHAR MTSO KHAR LOG NA PHA DANG AE 'PHRAD ZHUS PAS MI
'PHRAD CING BAR CHAD CHE BA 'DUG GSUNGS, PHA'I BLON PO THA'I
CANG GIS NGA 'DI NAS MGYOGS PAR MTSO KHAR PHYIN NA DPON PO
DANG AE MJAL, SDE RNAMS 'TSAM POR AE YOD, DPON SKU KHAMS

AE BZANG ZHUS PAS, DA LTA SDE YANG 'TSAM POR YOD, DPON YANG
SKU KHAMS BZANG BAR 'DUG ,KHYOD DANG DPON MI MJAL GSUNGS,
THA'I CANG GI BSAM PA LA, DPON SKU KHAMS BZANG, SDE 'TSAM POR
YOD NA ZLA BA GNYIS GSUM LA

KHRI PHRAG BZHI TZAM GYI ZANG ZING GI BDOG PA BSKUR BAR MDZAD,
SNGON NAS ZHAL BZHES YOD PA LTAR LHA SRAS BZHI PAS MTHUN RKYEN
SBYAR TE,

SKU GDUNG MCHOD RTEN RGYU DANG BZO DBYIBS, PHRA BKOD SOGS PHUN
SUM TSOGS PA ZHIG BSGRUBS TE BSKUR BA ZLA BA LNGA PA'I NANG DU
'BYOR, CHOS RJE RNAM PAS THUGS KHUR BZHES TE SKU GDUNG GI RING
BSREL RNAMS MCHOD RTEN GYI

NANG DU SPYAN DRANGS SHING GZUNGS 'JUG SOGS DAM PA GONG MA'I
PHYAG LEN DANG MTHUN PAR PHUL NAS RAB TU GNAS PA MDZAD DE,
BYIN RLABS KYI GZI 'OD YONGS SU 'BAR BA'I MCHOD SDONG DAM PA
SKYE DGU'I BSOD NAMS KYI ZHING DU

@120B LEGS PAR BSGRUB PAR MDZAD DO, ,SMRAS PA, THUGS BSKYED
BDUD RTZI'I MTSO CHEN DPAG DKA' BA, ,BRTZE CHEN NOR RGYAS
DBANG POS YONGS BZUNG STE, ,SMON LAM RI BOS BSRUBS PA'I NGO
MTSAR LAS, ,

RGYAL SRAS CHU SHEL DBANG PO DENG 'DIR 'KHRUNGS, ,GANGS CAN
MDO SMAD GSER LDAN DGA' MA'I BZHIN, ,SPRUL BA'I SKYES MCHOG
NYIN BYED DANG 'GROGS PA, ,DE YI MOD LA NYES BRGYA'I RGUD PA
YI, ,MUN PA'I BLA

GOS GLO BUR NYID DU DOR, ,THUB PA'I BSTAN LA RJES CHAGS DED
DPON KHYOD, ,DBUS GTZANG CHOS KYI RGYA MTSOR BDER BYON TE,
,GZHUNG LUGS NOR BU'I GAN MDZOD RNAM DPYOD KYI, ,GRU GZINGS
STONG

PHRAG G-YO BAS BDAG GIR MDZAD, ,RAB DKAR GRAGS PA'I AUTPAL
PHON PO NI, ,PHYOGS KYI BU MO'I RNA BAR BKOD BYAS PA, ,DE TSE
MKHAS RNAMS KHYOD ZHABS GUS BSNYEN TE, ,ZAB RGYAS MAN NGAG
'THUNGS

BAS CI YANG BREL, ,KHYOD ZHABS SEN MO'I 'DAB 'PHRENG RI BONG
CAN, ,BKRA SHIS DGE MTSAN 'OD ZER SPRO BA GANG, ,'KHOR BSGYUR
MGRIN SNGON RAL BAS GUS BSTEN NA, ,DREGS LDAN PHAL GYIS BTUD

'DIR CI ZHIG MTSAR, ,RGYU 'BRAS THEG BA'I DKA' GNAD MA LUS PA,
,GSAL BAR 'GREL BA'I KHYOD GSUNG LEGS BSHAD TSOGS, ,SKAL BZANG
SNYING GI YOL GOR BSTEN PA LAS, ,DUS MTHAR THUB

@121A *, ,BSTAN MDZES PA'I RGYAN DU GYUR, ,KHYOD KYI 'PHRIN
LAS DPAG BSAM SHING CHEN LAS, ,BSDU BZHI'I 'BRAS BU CHAR DU
BSNYIL BA YIS, ,THAR 'DOD LEGS BRIS TSOGS RNAMS KUN

DGA'I DBYANGS, ,SGROGS PAS SRID ZHI'I GDUNG BA SEL BA SNYAM,
,ZHES PA NI YONGS RDZOGS BSTAN PA'I MNGA' BDAG NGAG DBANG BLO
BZANG CHOS LDAN DPAL BZANG POR SKU'I SKYE BA BZHES PA'I YAL
'DAB STE BCU

BZHI PA'O, ,DE LTAR NA RJE BTZUN BLA MA THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA
LCANG SKYA ROL PA'I RDO RJE'I 'KHRUNGS RABS KYI 'PHRENG BA
GTAM TU BRJOD PA NGO MTSAR DAD PA'I LJON SHING ZHES BYA BA LAS
SKU TSE SNGA MA RNAMS KYI RNAM PAR THAR

PA BRJOD ZIN TO, ,ZHES PA 'DI NI RJE BTZUN BLA MA GANG GI
ZHABS 'BRING DU 'KHOD PA LUGS GNYIS LA BLO GROS KYI 'JUG BA
MCHOG TU YANGS PA'I AEM CHI CHOS RJE BLO BZANG RNAM RGYAL GYIS
MDZOD BTAGS, DNGUL GYI

MAndAL, GOS CHEN SER PO 'DOM BRGYAD YUG BCAS BSKUL BA LA BRTEN
NAS, RJE BTZUN BLA MA THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA GANG DE'I ZHABS KYI
PADMO LA NYE BAR GTUGS PA'I BTZUN PA ^ DKON MCHOG 'JIGS MED
DBANG PO'I

SDES GDONG NGAN ZHES PA ME SPREL HOR ZLA GNYIS PA'I TSES LA
SBYAR BA'I YI GE PA NI SNGAGS RAM PA CHOS 'DZIN DAR RGYAS SO,
,'DI LA LJAGS ZHUS SONG BA ZHIG YOD KYANG PHYAG DPE MA SNYUNG?
BAS THOR BU 'GA' BA SDUR NAS BRIS,
